         +ent floating overlay, Rust backend for process management, Reac
         +t 19 frontend with Tailwind CSS 4, real-time NDJSON streaming f
         +rom agent subprocess, permission server for human-in-the-loop t
         +ool approval

         +w for CLI login (`8gent auth login`), macOS Keychain token stor
         +age with AES-256-GCM encrypted file fallback, JWT validation vi
         +a `jose`, automatic token refresh, non-blocking anonymous mode 
         +(auth never blocks local usage)                                
      17 +- **`packages/db/` ‚ÄĒ Convex database** ‚ÄĒ reactive database with
         + users, sessions, usage, and preferences tables; real-time sync
         +; Clerk auth integration; offline mutation queuing; ConvexClien
         +t wrapper for Bun                                              
      18 +- **`packages/voice/` ‚ÄĒ Speech-to-Text via Whisper** ‚ÄĒ local tr
         +anscription via whisper.cpp CLI (no cloud dependency), sox-base
         +d mic recording, model manager with streaming downloads from Hu
         +gging Face (tiny/base/small), voice activity detection, OpenAI

         +ant provisioning with subdomain routing (username.8gent.app), u
         +sage analytics, billing plan definitions (free/pro/team), Strip
         +e integration stubs, admin dashboard data layer

      921 +  private _convexSessionId: string | null = null;             
      922 +                                                              
      923 +  private async _trackSessionStart(model: string, runtime: str
          +ing): Promise<void> {                                         
      924 +    try {                                                     
      925 +      const { getConvexClient } = await import("../../packages
          +/db/client.js");                                              
      926 +      const client = getConvexClient();                       
      927 +      // @ts-ignore ‚ÄĒ dynamic import of Convex API            
      928 +      const { api } = await import("../../packages/db/convex/_
          +generated/api.js");                                           
      929 +      const result = await client.mutation(api.sessions.start,
          + {                                                            
      930 +        model: model || "unknown",                            
      931 +        provider: runtime || "ollama",                        
      932 +      });                                                     
      933 +      if (result) this._convexSessionId = result;             
      934 +    } catch {                                                 
      935 +      // DB not available ‚ÄĒ silent, never blocks agent        
      936 +    }                                                         
      937 +  }                                                           
      938 +                                                              
      939 +  private async _trackSessionEnd(): Promise<void> {           
      940 +    if (!this._convexSessionId) return;                       
      941 +    try {                                                     
      942 +      const { getConvexClient } = await import("../../packages
          +/db/client.js");                                              
      943 +      const client = getConvexClient();                       
      944 +      const { api } = await import("../../packages/db/convex/_
          +generated/api.js");                                           
      945 +      await client.mutation(api.sessions.end, {               
      946 +        sessionId: this._convexSessionId,                     
      947 +        tokensUsed: this.totalTokensUsed || 0,                
      948 +        toolCalls: this.turnNumber || 0,                      
      949 +      });                                                     
      950 +    } catch {                                                 
      951 +      // Silent ‚ÄĒ never blocks cleanup                        
      952 +    }                                                         
      953 +  }                                                           
      954 +                                                              
      955    async cleanup(): Promise<void> {
      956 +    // Track session end in Convex                            
      957 +    await this._trackSessionEnd().catch(() => {});            
      958      // Stop heartbeat agents
      959      this.heartbeat.stop();

‚Źļ Here's what you can test right now:

  1. TUI (main experience)

  bun run tui
  Then try:
  - /auth status ‚ÄĒ should show "Not logged in"
  - /voice status ‚ÄĒ should report whisper available, sox missing
  - /help ‚ÄĒ should show auth and voice commands
  - Type a coding prompt ‚ÄĒ agent will run on your Eight models

  2. CLI Auth

  bun run bin/8gent.ts auth status    # shows current state
  bun run bin/8gent.ts auth login     # starts device flow (needs Clerk keys 
  first)
  Auth login won't work yet ‚ÄĒ needs Clerk keys in config. But the flow is wired.

  3. Voice (partial)

  Whisper is installed but sox is missing. To get full voice:
  brew install sox
  Then in the TUI, /voice record or Ctrl+Space will work.

  4. CLUI Desktop App

  Needs Tauri + Rust toolchain:
  # If you don't have Rust:
  curl --proto '=https' --tlsv1.2 -sSf https://sh.rustup.rs | sh
  # Then:
  cd apps/clui && bun install && bun run tauri dev

  5. Admin Dashboard

  Needs Convex project + Clerk keys:
  cd apps/dashboard && bun install && bun run dev
  Won't have data until Convex is deployed.

  closed it, relaunch with:

  cd ~/8gent-code/apps/clui && export PATH="$HOME/.cargo/bin:$PATH" && npx

  Three ways to toggle theme:
  - Click the ‚óź Dark / ‚óĎ Light button in the title bar
  - Cmd+Shift+T keyboard shortcut (cycles dark ‚Üí light ‚Üí system)
  - /theme light or /theme dark or /theme system command

  The "system" mode follows your macOS appearance setting automatically. Theme
  preference persists in localStorage.

‚Źļ No, it's not fully functional yet. Right now the CLUI is a visual scaffold ‚ÄĒ
  the UI renders but:

  1. Input doesn't connect to the agent ‚ÄĒ messages go to a mock handler, not
  packages/eight
  2. No subprocess spawning ‚ÄĒ the Rust backend has the code to spawn bun run 
  packages/eight/index.ts but it's not wired to the React frontend
  3. No NDJSON streaming ‚ÄĒ agent events aren't flowing to the UI
  4. Slash commands like /auth, /model just echo back instead of doing anything

  The reference CLUI-CC works because it spawns claude -p --output-format 
  stream-json as a subprocess and pipes NDJSON events. We need to do the same
  with our agent.

  The input issue you're seeing ‚ÄĒ can you type at all in the input field? If the
   cursor isn't appearing, it might be the decorations: true change interfering
  with focus. Can you share what happens when you click on the input area?

  The next step to make it actually functional is to wire the Tauri IPC commands
   (create_session, send_to_agent) from the React frontend so typing a message
  actually spawns and talks to the 8gent agent. Want me to do that now?

‚Źļ Good progress ‚ÄĒ the session IS creating (session_1), which means the Rust IPC
  is working. The Connected: No means the bridge subprocess started but its
  NDJSON events aren't reaching the frontend yet. Let me check what's happening
  in the terminal output.

  To answer your question about sessions:

  Current model (v0.6.0):
  - Each CLUI tab spawns its own bun run clui-bridge.ts subprocess
  - The session ID (session_1, session_2, etc.) is Rust-generated, local to that
   CLUI instance
  - No auth tie-in yet ‚ÄĒ it's a local process, same as running bun run tui

  Target model (with auth wired):
  - 8gent auth login ‚Üí Clerk device flow ‚Üí JWT stored in Keychain
  - Session starts ‚Üí JWT passed to Convex ‚Üí sessions.start({ userId, model, 
  provider })
  - Each session tracked in Convex with token usage, tool calls, duration
  - The CLUI session ID maps to a Convex session record via the auth user
  - Multiple devices (CLUI on laptop, TUI on server) all share the same user
  account

  So yes ‚ÄĒ unique session ID per tab, linked to your Clerk user when
  authenticated, persisted in Convex. Anonymous mode works without auth (just no
   cloud sync).

‚Źļ The bridge IS running (PID 86206). So the issue is that the Rust NDJSON reader

‚Źļ Read 1 file (ctrl+o to expand)

‚Źļ The code looks correct ‚ÄĒ connectTab is called inside init() which first sets
  up listen() then calls connectTab(). The issue might be that the session_start
   event is emitted by Rust in create_session BEFORE the subprocess stdout
  thread has a chance to emit it. Let me check ‚ÄĒ actually there are TWO
  session_start events: one from Rust (in create_session) and one from the
  bridge (NDJSON). The Rust one is emitted inline, before the subprocess thread
  runs.

  Wait, looking at the Rust code, the session_start event IS emitted at the
  bottom of create_session():

  let _ = app.emit("agent_event", &SessionEvent {
      session_id: session_id.clone(),
      event: AgentEvent { event_type: "session_start".to_string(), ... },
  });

  This should be received. The issue is that connectTab sets sessionId AFTER the
   event is emitted, so when the event arrives, the tab lookup fails because
  sessionId is still null at that point.

  The fix: set the sessionId on the tab BEFORE calling create_session, or handle
   the session_start event matching by the session ID returned from
  create_session.

  Actually the simpler fix ‚ÄĒ just set isConnected: true directly when
  create_session returns successfully:
